posted:Posted May 12, 2024
msg:This is my first time in Changsha. Howard Johnson's all-round service has given me an inexplicable fondness for this city. I booked a deluxe river view king room based on reviews on Ctrip. Xiao Wang has been very patient in communicating with me about the room requirements, check-in period, etc., and the check-in was indeed very well arranged according to my requirements. The hotel is very comfortable to stay in. The river view room has a wide view and unbeatable scenery. The breakfast is rich and tastes good. Because the high-speed rail leaves at 4 pm, I negotiated with the front desk whether the check-out time can be postponed to 2 pm. Xiao Wu at the front desk also enthusiastically helped coordinate to postpone the check-out to 2 pm, so that I can rest for two more hours in the hotel and avoid the fatigue of waiting at the station. Next time I come to Changsha, I will definitely choose to stay at Howard Johnson. Thanks again to Howard Johnson, thank you Xiao Wang and Xiao Wu for your warm and thoughtful arrangements, thank you!
